\documentclass[11pt]{article}
		\setcounter{section}{-1}
    \usepackage[breakable]{tcolorbox}
    \usepackage{parskip} % Stop auto-indenting (to mimic markdown behaviour)
    
    \usepackage{iftex}
    \ifPDFTeX
    	\usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    	\usepackage{mathpazo}
    \else
    	\usepackage{fontspec}
    \fi

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % Maintain compatibility with old templates. Remove in nbconvert 6.0
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionFormat{nocaption}{}
    \captionsetup{format=nocaption,aboveskip=0pt,belowskip=0pt}

    \usepackage{float}
    \floatplacement{figure}{H} % forces figures to be placed at the correct location
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range
    \makeatletter % fix for old versions of grffile with XeLaTeX
    \@ifpackagelater{grffile}{2019/11/01}
    {
      % Do nothing on new versions
    }
    {
      \def\Gread@@xetex#1{%
        \IfFileExists{"\Gin@base".bb}%
        {\Gread@eps{\Gin@base.bb}}%
        {\Gread@@xetex@aux#1}%
      }
    }
    \makeatother
    \usepackage[Export]{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size
    \adjustboxset{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}

    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    % The default LaTeX title has an obnoxious amount of whitespace. By default,
    % titling removes some of it. It also provides customization options.
    \usepackage{titling}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines
    \usepackage{mathrsfs}
    

    
    % Colors for the hyperref package

    \definecolor{citecolor}{rgb}{.12,.54,.11}

    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}

\def\PY@toks#1+{\ifx\relax#1\empty\else%
    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

    % For linebreaks inside Verbatim environment from package fancyvrb. 
    \makeatletter
        \newbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox 
        \newbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedvisiblespace {\textcolor{red}{\textvisiblespace}} 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol {\textcolor{red}{\llap{\tiny$\m@th\hookrightarrow$}}} 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationindent {3ex } 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedafterbreak {\kern\Wrappedcontinuationindent\copy\Wrappedcontinuationbox} 
        % Take advantage of the already applied Pygments mark-up to insert 
        % potential linebreaks for TeX processing. 
        %        {, <, #, %, $, ' and ": go to next line. 
        %        _, }, ^, &, >, - and ~: stay at end of broken line. 
        % Use of \textquotesingle for straight quote. 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatspecials {% 
            \def\PYGZus{\discretionary{\char`\_}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\_}}% 
            \def\PYGZob{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\{}{\char`\{}}% 
            \def\PYGZcb{\discretionary{\char`\}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\}}}% 
            \def\PYGZca{\discretionary{\char`\^}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\^}}% 
            \def\PYGZam{\discretionary{\char`\&}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\&}}% 
            \def\PYGZlt{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\<}{\char`\<}}% 
            \def\PYGZgt{\discretionary{\char`\>}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\>}}% 
            \def\PYGZsh{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\#}{\char`\#}}% 
            \def\PYGZpc{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\%}{\char`\%}}% 
            \def\PYGZdl{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\$}{\char`\$}}% 
            \def\PYGZhy{\discretionary{\char`\-}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\-}}% 
            \def\PYGZsq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\textquotesingle}{\textquotesingle}}% 
            \def\PYGZdq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\"}{\char`\"}}% 
            \def\PYGZti{\discretionary{\char`\~}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\~}}% 
        } 
        % Some characters . , ; ? ! / are not pygmentized. 
        % This macro makes them "active" and they will insert potential linebreaks 
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatpunct {% 
            \lccode`\~`\.\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\.}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\.}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\,\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\,}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\,}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\;\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\;}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\;}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\:\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\:}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\:}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\?\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\?}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\?}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\!\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\!}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\!}}}% 
            \lccode`\~`\/\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\/}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\/}}}% 
            \catcode`\.\active
            \catcode`\,\active 
            \catcode`\;\active
            \catcode`\:\active
            \catcode`\?\active
            \catcode`\!\active
            \catcode`\/\active 
            \lccode`\~`\~ 	
        }
    \makeatother

    \let\OriginalVerbatim=\Verbatim
    \makeatletter
    \renewcommand{\Verbatim}[1][1]{%
        %\parskip\z@skip
        \sbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox {\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol}%
        \sbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox {\FV@SetupFont\Wrappedvisiblespace}%
        \def\FancyVerbFormatLine ##1{\hsize\linewidth
            \vtop{\raggedright\hyphenpenalty\z@\exhyphenpenalty\z@
                \doublehyphendemerits\z@\finalhyphendemerits\z@
                \strut ##1\strut}%
        }%
        % If the linebreak is at a space, the latter will be displayed as visible
        % space at end of first line, and a continuation symbol starts next line.
        % Stretch/shrink are however usually zero for typewriter font.
        \def\FV@Space {%
            \nobreak\hskip\z@ plus\fontdimen3\font minus\fontdimen4\font
            \discretionary{\copy\Wrappedvisiblespacebox}{\Wrappedafterbreak}
            {\kern\fontdimen2\font}%
        }%
        
        % Allow breaks at special characters using \PYG... macros.
        \Wrappedbreaksatspecials
        % Breaks at punctuation characters . , ; ? ! and / need catcode=\active 	
        \OriginalVerbatim[#1,codes*=\Wrappedbreaksatpunct]%
    }
    \makeatother

    \definecolor{incolor}{HTML}{303F9F}
    \definecolor{outcolor}{HTML}{D84315}
    \definecolor{cellborder}{HTML}{CFCFCF}
    \definecolor{cellbackground}{HTML}{F7F7F7}
    
    % prompt
    \makeatletter
    \newcommand{\boxspacing}{\kern\kvtcb@left@rule\kern\kvtcb@boxsep}
    \makeatother
    \newcommand{\prompt}[4]{
        {\ttfamily\llap{{\color{#2}[#3]:\hspace{3pt}#4}}\vspace{-\baselineskip}}
    }
    

    
    % Prevent overflowing lines due to hard-to-break entities
    \sloppy 
    % Setup hyperref package
    \hypersetup{
      breaklinks=true,  % so long urls are correctly broken across lines
      colorlinks=true,
      urlcolor=urlcolor,
      linkcolor=linkcolor,
      citecolor=citecolor,
      }
    % Slightly bigger margins than the latex defaults

    \hypertarget{introduction-to-programming-review}{%
\section{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{INTRODUCTION TO PROGRAMMING
REVIEW}}{INTRODUCTION TO PROGRAMMING REVIEW}}\label{introduction-to-programming-review}}

\textbf{\emph{Written by Hoang Tran Nhat Minh,}}

Hanoi University of Science and Technology,

Data Science and Artificial Intelligence - K65.

\textbf{Guided by Dr.~Dinh Viet Sang.}

    \hypertarget{preface}{%
\subsection{PREFACE}\label{preface}}

    \textbf{Thank you, my teacher, Dr.~Dinh Viet Sang, I cannot learn
programming in Python that much without you. This notebook uses a huge
part your lectures as a guidance.}

\emph{Dear Data Science \& AI - K65,}

This is my last notebook in order to prepare for the final exam on
Introduction to Programming. If you find this notebook helpful, thanks
for reading it. Some might find this one not that helpful, I highly
appreciate every line of text you read, including this one.

If you find any mistake, feedback and I will try to fix it as soon as
possible.

Thank y'all for supporting me all the time, good luck on all of your
exams.

Best wishes,

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}/content/sample\PYZus{}data/README.md}
\PY{n}{f} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{f}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{read}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{f}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{close}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Name = /content/sample\_data/README.md
This directory includes a few sample datasets to get you started.

*   `california\_housing\_data*.csv` is California housing data from the 1990 US
    Census; more information is available at:
    https://developers.google.com/machine-learning/crash-course/california-
housing-data-description

*   `mnist\_*.csv` is a small sample of the
    [MNIST database](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MNIST\_database), which is
    described at: http://yann.lecun.com/exdb/mnist/

*   `anscombe.json` contains a copy of
    [Anscombe's quartet](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anscombe\%27s\_quartet); it
    was originally described in

    Anscombe, F. J. (1973). 'Graphs in Statistical Analysis'. American
    Statistician. 27 (1): 17-21. JSTOR 2682899.

    and our copy was prepared by the
    [vega\_datasets library](https://github.com/altair-viz/vega\_datasets/blob/4f6
7bdaad10f45e3549984e17e1b3088c731503d/vega\_datasets/\_data/anscombe.json).

    \end{Verbatim}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{two\PYZus{}time}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{number}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} docstring}
    \PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZsq{}\PYZsq{}\PYZsq{}}
\PY{l+s+sd}{    2 times a number}
\PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZsq{}\PYZsq{}\PYZsq{}}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} body}
    \PY{n}{doubled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{2} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{number}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} returns (if not, it is a void function)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{doubled}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} function call, pass argument(s) to parameter(s)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{two\PYZus{}time}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{8}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{two\PYZus{}time}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n+nv+vm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}doc\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \hypertarget{pass-by-object-reference}{%
\subsection{PASS-BY-OBJECT-REFERENCE}\label{pass-by-object-reference}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{14}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} PASS\PYZhy{}BY\PYZhy{}OBJECT\PYZhy{}REFERENCE}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Immutable objects: int, float, complex, string, tuple, frozen set, bytes}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Mutable objects: list, dict, set, byte array}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{change\PYZus{}num}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{num} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
\PY{n}{a} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{4}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{a}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{change\PYZus{}num}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{a}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{a}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{change\PYZus{}lst}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lst}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{lst}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{changed}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{l} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{original}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{l}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{change\PYZus{}lst}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{l}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{l}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
4
4
['original']
['original', 'changed']
    \end{Verbatim}

\subsection{SCOPE}\label{scope}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{15}{\boxspacing}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{f}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{In f:    x =}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{First:   x =}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{After f: x =}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

In f:    x = 1
After f: x = 0
    \end{Verbatim}

        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{0! = 1}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{pr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
7! = 6! * 7
6! = 5! * 6
5! = 4! * 5
4! = 3! * 4
3! = 2! * 3
2! = 1! * 2
1! = 0! * 1
0! = 1
5040
    \end{Verbatim}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} print the initialized board}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{print\PYZus{}board}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} run, print the board every move and return the result}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s1}{Number of transfers: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}i}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}} \PY{n}{hanoi\PYZus{}tower}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} n SHOULD BE LESS THAN 5}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

\paragraph{MapReduce APPLICATION: COUNT NUMBER OF A
WORD}\label{mapreduce-application-count-number-of-a-word}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{62}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} MapReduce APPLICATION: COUNT NUMBER OF A WORD}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} count the number of the word \PYZdq{}the\PYZdq{}/\PYZdq{}The\PYZdq{} in a sentence}
\PY{n}{text} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{The word }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{deep}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ in }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{deep learning}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ refers to the number of layers through which the data is transformed. More precisely, deep learning systems have a substantial credit assignment path (CAP) depth. The CAP is the chain of transformations from input to output. CAPs describe potentially causal connections between input and output. For a feedforward neural network, the depth of the CAPs is that of the network and is the number of hidden layers plus one (as the output layer is also parameterized). For recurrent neural networks, in which a signal may propagate through a layer more than once, the CAP depth is potentially unlimited.[2] No universally agreed\PYZhy{}upon threshold of depth divides shallow learning from deep learning, but most researchers agree that deep learning involves CAP depth higher than 2. CAP of depth 2 has been shown to be a universal approximator in the sense that it can emulate any function.[15] Beyond that, more layers do not add to the function approximator ability of the network. Deep models (CAP \PYZgt{} 2) are able to extract better features than shallow models and hence, extra layers help in learning the features effectively.}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
\PY{n}{ifThe} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k}{lambda} \PY{n}{word}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{word} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{the}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{The}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{k}{else} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{reduce}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sumof2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{map}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{ifThe}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{text}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}

            \PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{i}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{lst}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}


\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{random} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{randint}
\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}list} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{randint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{15}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}list}\PY{p}{)}

    \hypertarget{chapter-8-object-oriented-programming-oop}{%
\section{CHAPTER 8: OBJECT-ORIENTED PROGRAMMING
(OOP)}\label{chapter-8-object-oriented-programming-oop}}

    \hypertarget{create-a-new-object-example}{%
\subsection{CREATE A NEW OBJECT
EXAMPLE}\label{create-a-new-object-example}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{104}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} CREATE A NEW OBJECT EXAMPLE}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}     name of class (parent class(es))}
\PY{k}{class} \PY{n+nc}{Complex\PYZus{}number}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{object}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{} always run right after calling the class}
    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{a}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{b}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} real and imaginary are attributes}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{real} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{a}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imaginary} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{b}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} a method is a function of the class}
    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{modulus}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{math} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{sqrt}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{real} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imaginary} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZus{}\PYZus{}str\PYZus{}\PYZus{} is a method which returns (str(an instance))}
    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}str\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Complex number (}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}s}\PY{l+s+s1}{ + }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}s}\PY{l+s+s1}{i)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{real}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imaginary}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZus{}\PYZus{}add\PYZus{}\PYZus{} is a method which returns (an instance + another instance)}
    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}add\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{other}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{Complex\PYZus{}number}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{real} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{other}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{real}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imaginary} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{other}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imaginary}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZus{}\PYZus{}sub\PYZus{}\PYZus{} is a method which returns (an instance \PYZhy{} another instance)}
    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}sub\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{other}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{Complex\PYZus{}number}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{real} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{other}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{real}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imaginary} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{other}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imaginary}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZus{}\PYZus{}eq\PYZus{}\PYZus{} is a method which returns (an instance == another instance)}
    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}eq\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{other}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{real} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{other}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{real} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imaginary} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{other}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imaginary}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    The most common used methods for a class, in short:

\begin{verbatim}
__doc__: docstring  |  __name__: name  |  __del__: delete
__lt__: "<"  |  __le__: "<="  |  __ne__: "!="
__gt__: ">"  |  __ge__: ">="
__dir__: dir(an object or an instance)
\end{verbatim}

\begin{verbatim}
object.__add__(self, other)
object.__sub__(self, other)
object.__mul__(self, other)
object.__matmul__(self, other)
object.__truediv__(self, other)
object.__floordiv__(self, other)
object.__mod__(self, other)
object.__divmod__(self, other)
object.__pow__(self, other[, modulo])
object.__lshift__(self, other)
object.__rshift__(self, other)
object.__and__(self, other)
object.__xor__(self, other)
object.__or__(self, other)
\end{verbatim}

There are so many more methods for a class that you should find them out
yourself, this is the documentation of data model in Python:

\url{https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html}

I found that the @abstractmethod decorator is not really important for
the final exam, since we didn't learn any thing about decorator in
Python, so if you are curious enough, this is the documentation of abc:

\url{https://docs.python.org/3/library/abc.html}

\PY{k}{class} \PY{n+nc}{Imaginary\PYZus{}number}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Complex\PYZus{}number}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:} 
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{removed\PYZus{}real\PYZus{}part} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{None}
            \PY{n}{imaginary\PYZus{}part} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} len(args) == 2}
            \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{removed\PYZus{}real\PYZus{}part} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{n}{imaginary\PYZus{}part} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 2 ways to initialize:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} super().\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}(0, imaginary\PYZus{}part)}
        \PY{n}{Complex\PYZus{}number}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{imaginary\PYZus{}part}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}str\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Imaginary number (}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}s}\PY{l+s+s1}{i)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imaginary}\PY{p}{)}

    \hypertarget{chapter-9-testing-debugging-exceptions-and-assertions}{%
\section{CHAPTER 9: TESTING, DEBUGGING, EXCEPTIONS AND

    \hypertarget{testing-and-debugging}{%
\subsection{TESTING AND DEBUGGING}\label{testing-and-debugging}}

    By now, you have done this every time an error occurs in your code, so
this is pretty both too easy and too hard to be explained in this
notebook. Therefore, I will not explain about it here.

    \hypertarget{exceptions}{%
\subsection{EXCEPTIONS}\label{exceptions}}

    \hypertarget{common-built-in-exceptions}{%
\subsubsection{COMMON BUILT-IN
EXCEPTIONS}\label{common-built-in-exceptions}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{112}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} COMMON BUILT\PYZhy{}IN EXCEPTIONS}
\PY{n}{lst} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{verbatim}
print(lst[4])
IndexError: list index out of range

print(int(lst))
TypeError: int() argument must be a string, a bytes-like object or a number, not 'list'

print(an_undefined_a_variable)
NameError: name 'an_undefined_a_variable' is not defined

print(a

    print(a
           ^
SyntaxError: unexpected EOF while parsing

print(lst.mnpq)
AttributeError: 'list' object has no attribute 'mnpq'

print(6 / 0)
ZeroDivisionError: division by zero

print(int('?'))
ValueError: invalid literal for int() with base 10: '?'

f = open('????')
FileNotFoundError: [Errno 2] No such file or directory: '????'
\end{verbatim}

    \hypertarget{input-handling-specific-exceptions}{%
\subsubsection{(INPUT) HANDLING SPECIFIC
EXCEPTIONS}\label{input-handling-specific-exceptions}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{113}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} HANDLING SPECIFIC EXCEPTIONS}
\PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{a} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{a = }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{b} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{b = }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{res} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{a} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{b}

\PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{ValueError}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Handling a specific exception in try clause}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Unable to convert to number}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{ZeroDivisionError}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Unable to divide by 0}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{except}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Handling any other exception in try clause}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Another error}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Only execute if the try clause does not raise any exception}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{res}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{finally}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Always execute}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Done}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
a = 4
b = 8
0.5
Done
    \end{Verbatim}

    \begin{verbatim}
a = sfgopsgspg
Unable to convert to number
Done

a = 4
b = 0
Unable to divide by 0
Done

a = 4
b = 8
0.5
Done
\end{verbatim}

\end{verbatim}

    \hypertarget{input-define-an-exception}{%
\subsubsection{(INPUT) DEFINE AN
EXCEPTION}\label{input-define-an-exception}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{114}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} DEFINE AN EXCEPTION}
\PY{k}{class} \PY{n+nc}{DateFormatError}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+ne}{Exception}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{pass}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Raise the exception if the string is not of the format \PYZsq{}??\PYZhy{}??\PYZhy{}????\PYZsq{}}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ? is a number, from 0\PYZhy{}9}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{num\PYZus{}args\PYZus{}check}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{date}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{dmy\PYZus{}lst} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{date}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dmy\PYZus{}lst}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{k+kc}{True}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{k+kc}{False}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{numeric\PYZus{}check}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{date}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{dmy\PYZus{}lst} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{date}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{arg} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{dmy\PYZus{}lst}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{arg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{isnumeric}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{k}{return} \PY{k+kc}{False}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{k+kc}{True}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{args\PYZus{}len\PYZus{}check}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{date}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{dmy\PYZus{}lst} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{date}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{len\PYZus{}lst} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dmy\PYZus{}lst}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{tuple}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{len\PYZus{}lst}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{k+kc}{True}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{k+kc}{False}

\PY{n}{date} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Date = }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}args\PYZus{}check}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{date}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{raise} \PY{n}{DateFormatError}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{There must be 3 arguments for day\PYZhy{}month\PYZhy{}year, respectively}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{numeric\PYZus{}check}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{date}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{raise} \PY{n}{DateFormatError}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{At least one of 3 arguments is not numeric}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{args\PYZus{}len\PYZus{}check}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{date}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{raise} \PY{n}{DateFormatError}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{len() of 3 arguments must be 2, 2, 4, respectively}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{The date is: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}s}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}} \PY{n}{date}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Date = 66-99-6969
The date is: 66-99-6969
    \end{Verbatim}

    \begin{verbatim}

Date = 1-12-4251
DateFormatError: len() of 3 arguments must be 2, 2, 4, respectively

Date = 30-12-200x
DateFormatError: At least one of 3 arguments is not numeric

Date = 66-99-6969
The date is: 66-99-6969
\end{verbatim}

    \hypertarget{sequence}{%
\subsubsection{SEQUENCE}\label{sequence}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{117}{\boxspacing}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(} \PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{9}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{3.2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{2.1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{6.0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mf}{1.3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]} \PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} a list/tuple of lists/tuples of... is allowed}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{9}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dtype} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float} \PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} check it out in the documentation}
\end{Verbatim}
